Others: The souvenirs are exquisite, the breakfast has not many varieties, but the taste is very good.
Disadvantages: There is no wardrobe, only a small clothes hanger. There are many clothes in winter, and there is no place to hang them after they are taken off. The sockets are loose and the sound insulation is not good. If I could sum it up in one sentence, it can only be said that the hotel spent a lot of fancy design ideas but did not understand the guests' accommodation needs at all.
